本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Naval Architecture and Ocean Engineering Major
[2024级适用]
船舶与海洋工程（081901）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
船舶与海洋工程专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Naval Architecture and Ocean Engineering Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
船舶与海洋工程专业入选2020年度国家级一流本科专业建设点，专业立足海洋强国，学生主要学习数学、物理、力学、外语、计算机、绿色智能及船舶与海洋工程原理的基础知识；船舶与海洋结构物设计制造、船舶管理等专业基础知识；熟悉国内和国际有关船舶与海洋结构物的规范与法规；了解造船与海洋开发的理论前沿、新型船舶与海洋结构物的发展动态；掌握船舶与海洋结构物的设计、建造、经营的理论和方法，具有从事实际工作的能力和一定的科学研究的能力。
Naval Architecture and Marine Engineering major has been selected as a national first-class undergraduate major construction site in 2020.With a focus on building a strong maritime country,students will learn mathematics, physics, mechanics, foreign language, computer and basic knowledge about the principle of naval architecture and ocean engineering, design, manufacture and management of ship and ocean engineering structures; familiar with domestic and international norms and regulations about ship and ocean engineering structure ; understand the frontier theory on shipbuilding and ocean exploration and development tendency of new ship and ocean engineering structure; master theory and methods about design, manufacture, management of ship and ocean engineering structure; have the ability to engage in practical work and some scientific research.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业培养具备现代船舶与海洋工程设计制造基础理论、专业知识与应用能力，充分发挥大连海事大学航运特色，结合教学实习船和智能研究实训两用船，构建船舶知识体系，突出安全、绿色与智能船舶特色，能够在船舶与海洋结构物设计、制造、检验、使用、研究和管理等部门从事技术和管理方面工作，并在工程实践中遵守职业道德和规范，体现创新、法律、环境意识、团队合作协调能力与国际视野，通过不断学习和自我提升，具有创新素质和工程实践能力相结合的复合型专业拔尖人才。
The program aims to cultivate students who possess the basic theories, professional knowledge, and application abilities of modern ship and ocean engineering design and manufacturing, fully leverage the shipping characteristics of Dalian Maritime University, combine teaching internship ships and intelligent research and training dual-purpose ships, construct a ship knowledge system, highlight the characteristics of safety, green, and intelligent ships, be able to work in technical and management departments such as ship and ocean structure design, manufacturing, inspection, use, research, and management, and abide by professional ethics and norms in engineering practice, demonstrate innovation, legal, environmental awareness, team cooperation and coordination ability, and international perspective. Through continuous learning and self-improvement, students are top-notch professionals with a combination of innovative qualities and engineering practice abilities.

III．Graduation Requirements

造型与舱室设计、船舶三维建模仿真、船舶动力装置与系统、船舶电气系统设计、船舶工程优化设计方法 、计算机辅助船舶制造、船舶技术经济论证、计算机辅助船舶设计、船舶节能技术、船舶水动力数值模拟计算、船舶振动与噪声、船舶实习

后    记
培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，本年度培养计划在2021年修订版基础上做了微调。在多次校对、反复审核的过程当中，得到了各教学单位领导、教务、以及老师的大力支持和帮助。在此，对在培养计划修订过程中给予支持和帮助的各位，表示衷心的感谢。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

2024年9月
本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Mechanical Design & Manufacturing and Their Automation Major
[2024级适用]
机械设计制造及其自动化（080202）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
机械设计制造及其自动化专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Mechanical Design & Manufacturing and Their Automation Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
本专业是以“宽口径、厚基础、强能力、高素质”的创新型人才培养模式为办学思想，以机械工程为基础并与计算机、自动化、信息化、智能化等现代科学技术相结合，培养学生具备机械设计、制造和机电控制等基础知识与应用能力。学生就业范围广，毕业生可以到制造装备、船舶与海洋工程、汽车、航空航天、工程机械、电子仪表、石油化工、能源、建筑工程等领域从事机械装备设计、制造、服务以及生产管理工作。
Inspired by the education mode of innovative talents, the educational philosophy of this major is to cultivate students with broad employment prospects, solid foundation, strong ability and high quality. Based on mechanical engineering, and combined with modern science and technology such as computer, automation, information technology, and artificial intelligence, this major will make the students obtain the basic knowledge and application ability of mechanical design, manufacturing and mechatronic control. Students in this major have a wide range of employment. Graduates can engage in mechanical equipment design, manufacturing, service and production management in the fields of manufacturing equipment, ship and ocean engineering, automobile, aerospace, engineering machinery, electronic instrument, petrochemical industry, energy, construction engineering and other fields.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业培养具备机械设计制造及其自动化基础理论、专业知识与应用能力，能在机械工程领域从事设计和制造、技术开发、应用研究和运行管理等方面工作，并在工程实践中遵守职业道德和规范，富有创新、法律与环境意识，具有团队精神、持续学习能力与国际视野，能够成为德智体美劳全面发展的高素质工程技术人才，为社会主义事业培养优秀建设者和接班人。
上述培养目标可具体表述为以下四个子项：
培养目标 1：系统地运用数学与自然科学、机械专业基础知识，以及机械设计、制造、自动化技术等专业知识；能够从事设计制造、技术开发、应用研究和运行管理等方面工作；
培养目标 2：具备独立分析和解决机械领域复杂工程问题的能力，富有实践和创新能力，能够成为所在工作领域的高素质工程技术人才；
培养目标 3：具备高度的社会责任感和职业道德，德智体美劳全面发展，能在工程实践中全面考虑和评价社会、健康、安全、法律、环境及可持续发展等方面的问题，成为社会主义事业优秀的建设者和接班人；
培养目标 4：具有团队协作、组织协调和跨文化合作交流能力；具备自主和终身学习能力，不断提升自我，以适应社会经济发展的需要。
This major cultivates the students with the basic theory, professional knowledge and application ability of mechanical design, manufacturing and their automation. And students can engage in design and manufacturing, technology development, application research and operation management in the field of mechanical engineering, abide by professional ethics and norms in engineering practice, be full of innovation, legal and environmental awareness, team spirit, continuous learning ability and international perspective, and be able to become high-quality engineering and technical personnel with all-round development of morality, intelligence, physique, beauty and labor, and excellent builders and successors for the socialist cause.
The above program objectives can be specifically expressed as the following four sub-items:
Objective 1: Students systematically apply the basic knowledge of mathematics and natural science, machinery, as well as mechanical design, manufacturing, automation technology and other professional knowledge, and engage in design and manufacturing, technology development, application research and operation management, etc.;
Objective 2: Students have the ability to analyze and solve complex engineering problems in mechanical field independently, have the ability of practice and innovation, and be able to become high-quality engineering and technical personnel in their working field;
Objective 3: Students have a high sense of social responsibility and professional ethics, develop morally, intellectually, physically, aesthetically and laboriously in an all-round way, and be able to comprehensively consider and evaluate social, health, safety, law, environment and sustainable development in engineering practice, and become an excellent builder and successor of socialist cause;
Objective 4: Students have the ability of team work, organization, coordination, and cross-cultural cooperation & communication, and have the ability of self-learning and lifelong learning to constantly improve themselves to meet the needs of social and economic development.

III．Graduation requirements

2024年9月
本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Rescue and Salvage Engineering (Subsea Intelligent Equipment) Major
[2024级适用]
救助与打捞工程（081807T）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
救助与打捞工程（海洋智能装备）专业本科培养计划Undergraduate Program for Rescue and Salvage Engineering (Subsea Intelligent Equipment) Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
大连海事大学救助与打捞工程（海洋智能装备）专业（卓越工程师）成立于2009年，2011年获批进入教育部卓越工程师教育培养计划，2019年获批辽宁省一流本科教育示范专业建设点，2022年获批国家级一流本科专业建设点。目前招生规模为每年1个自然班，约30人。本专业现有专职教师27人，其中博士生导师10人、教授9人、副教授7人、讲师8人，本专业教师全部具有博士学位。另有专职实验教师3人。
救助与打捞工程专业是根据国家战略要求和救捞职责，以培养救捞卓越工程师为目标设立的本科专业。专业除船舶、航海学和海洋工程学等基础知识、船舶与海工机械的设计、结构、力学等学科知识外，设有潜水、救助工程、打捞工程、海洋工程服务、救捞政策法规和项目管理等特色课程，以及航海培训、船舶实习、救捞实践与工程训练等实践类课程群。本专业毕业生通过系统的课程学习和工程实践，能够从事救助工程、打捞工程、海洋工程等方面的设计制造、研究开发、指挥实施和管理等工作。
The department of Rescue and Salvage Engineering in Dalian Maritime University was originated founded in the 2009, and entered the Excellence Engineer Training Program in 2011. Approved as a first-class undergraduate education demonstration major construction site in Liaoning Province in 2019, and a national first-class undergraduate major construction site in 2022. At present, one class including about 30 students are admitted every year. The major currently consists of 27 full-time faculty members, including 10 doctoral supervisors, 9 professors, 7 associate professors and 8 lecturers, all of them have the doctor’s degree. In addition, there are 3 full-time experimental teachers.
The rescue and salvage engineering major is built for the national strategy and responsibility, aiming to implement the excellent engineers training plan. The program includes the basic knowledge on naval architecture, navigation, ocean engineering, mechanical engineering, mechanics, and special courses such as diving, rescue engineering, salvage engineering, ocean engineering, policy and laws of rescue and salvage, international standards contract, emergency management of salvage, project management of salvage engineering, etc. Practical courses such as maritime training, ship practice, rescue and salvage practice and engineering training are also strengthened. This program aims to cultivate students with systematic course study and engineering practice, to have the ability to design and manufacturer, research, direct and manage in enterprise and institutions for rescue and salvage engineering and ocean engineering.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业培养掌握现代化的海洋工程基本理论与技术，熟悉海洋技术智能化装备，了解海洋、海事相关的法律、法规，能在交通行业、海洋装备与技术设计研究单位、船舶行业、救助打捞行业以及海洋工程技术培训教育机构从事设计、研究、制造、管理等工作，并在工程实践中遵守职业道德和规范，体现创新、法律、环境意识、团队合作协调能力与国际视野，通过不断学习自我提升的高级专业技术人才，为社会主义事业培养优秀建设者和接班人。
This program aims to cultivate students with all around development of morality, intelligence, and physique. Understand the laws and regulations of salvage. Grasp the advanced technology and professional skills of salvage. Be familiar with salvaging equipment. Have the ability to design, research, manufacture, inspect, direct, manage and implement in the field of salvage system, kinds of ocean engineering company, the institute of salvaging equipment to research, design and manufacture, in design office, enterprise and educational institutions for salvage technical training, and cultivate excellent builders and successors for the socialist cause.
三、毕业要求
III．Graduation Requirements
本专业学生毕业时应掌握和具备以下几方面的知识与能力：
Our Graduate Attribute Profile has 12 elements, supported by a Knowledge Profile and a definition of the Level of Problem Solving, both given below:
工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础知识和专业知识应用于救助与打捞工程领域复杂工程问题的解决；
Engineering knowledge: Apply knowledge of rescue and salvage engineering based mathematics, natural science, engineering fundamentals and an engineering specialization respectively to the solution of complex engineering problems;
问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学、工程基础和救助与打捞工程基本原理以及通过文献研究来对救助与打捞工程领域的复杂工程问题进行识别、表达和研究分析，以获得有效结论；
Problem analysis: Identify, formulate, describe and analysis complex engineering problems reaching substantiated conclusions using first principles of mathematics, natural sciences and rescue and salvage engineering;
设计/开发解决方案：能够进行救助与打捞工程的全周期、全流程设计，或基于工程实际问题进行工艺流程或方案设计以解决复杂救助与打捞工程问题，并设计环节中体现出创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化、环境等问题；
Design/development of solutions: Design solutions for complex engineering problems and design new rescue and salvage engineering processes that meet specified needs with appropriate consideration for public health, and safety, cultural, societal and environmental considerations;
研究：能够基于救助与打捞工程基本原理并采用科学的方法通过设计、实施实验方案、分析、解释实验结果与数据对复杂的工程问题进行研究，并通过综合各方面的信息得出合理有效的结论；
Investigation: Conduct investigations of complex problems using fundamental knowledge of rescue and salvage engineering and research methods including design of experiments, analysis and interpretation of data, and synthesis of information to provide valid conclusions.
使用现代工具：能够在解决救助与打捞工程领域复杂工程问题时合理的使用和开发相关的技术、资源、程序、模拟软件、分析检测仪器、工程工具和信息技术工具等，并理解其局限性；
Modern tool usage: Have the good knowledge on the techniques, resources and modern engineering and IT tools regarding to the rescue and salvage engineering, and create, select and apply appropriate items, including prediction and modeling, to complex engineering problems;
工程与社会：能够基于救助与打捞工程领域相关的工程背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任；
The engineer and society: Apply reasoning informed by rescue and salvage engineering knowledge to assess societal, health, safety, legal and cultural issues and the consequent responsibilities relevant to material engineering practice and solutions to complex engineering problems;
环境与可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响；
Environment and sustainability: Understand and evaluate the sustainability and impact of engineering work in the solution of complex rescue and salvage engineering problems in societal and environmental contexts;
职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在救助与打捞工程领域的工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任；
Ethics: Apply ethical principles and commit to professional ethics and responsibilities and norms of rescue and salvage engineering practice;
个人和团队：具备良好的团队合作精神与责任意识，能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色；
Individual and teamwork: Function effectively as an individual, and as a member or leader in diverse teams and in multi-disciplinary settings;
沟通：能够就救助与打捞工程领域的复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流；
Communication: Communicate effectively on complex rescue and salvage engineering problems with the engineering community and society at large, such as being able to comprehend and write effective reports and design documentation, make effective presentations and give and receive clear instructions.
项目管理：理解并掌握救助与打捞工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用；
Project management and finance: Demonstrate knowledge and understanding of rescue and salvage engineering management principles and economic decision-making and apply these to one’s own work as a member and leader in a team, to manage projects and in multi-disciplinary environments.
终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。
Life-long learning: Recognize the need for, and have the preparation and ability to engage in, independent and life-long learning in the broadest context of technological change.
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
救助工程、打捞工程、海洋工程、潜水技术基础、救助与打捞政策法规、救捞国际标准合同、救捞应急管理、工程项目管理、救捞专业英语。
Rescue Engineering, Salvage Engineering, Ocean Engineering, Basics of Diving Technology, Policy and Laws of Rescue and Salvage, International Standards Contract, Emergency Management of Salvage, Project management, Rescue and salvage English.

后    记
培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，本年度培养计划在2021年修订版基础上做了微调。在多次校对、反复审核的过程当中，得到了各教学单位领导、教务、以及老师的大力支持和帮助。在此，对在培养计划修订过程中给予支持和帮助的各位，表示衷心的感谢。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Energy and Power Engineering Major
[2024级适用]
能源与动力工程（080501）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
能源与动力工程专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Energy and Power Engineering Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
大连海事大学能源与动力工程专业成立于2006年，本专业现有专任教师19人，其中教授6人（均为博士生导师）、副教授7人、讲师6人，19人具有博士学位。另有专职实验教师1人。
能源与动力工程专业坚持“开拓、创新、进取、卓越”的人才培养理念，是培养节能、动力和环保领域的宽口径、高水平人才的摇篮。学生就业范围广，能在能源、环保、石油化工、航空航天、空调与制冷、动力等相关领域从事研发、设计、制造、安装、运行、管理、营销等工作，也可以在科研院所、高等学校、政府机关等单位从事科研、教学与管理等相关工作。
专业经过交通运输部“十一五”、“十二五”重点实验室建设和“211工程”三期重点学科建设，拥有船用小型燃气轮机技术重点实验室，专业建设规模、实验条件和研究能力已达到国内大学同类专业的先进水平。
The major of energy and power engineering of Dalian Maritime University was founded in 2006. There are 19 full-time teachers in the major, including 6 professors (all doctoral supervisors), 7 associate professors, 6 lecturers, and 19 of them have the doctor’s degree. There is also one full-time experimental teacher.
Energy and power engineering, insisting on the talents cultivation of “Pioneering, Innovation, Enterprise, Excellence”, is a cradle for the wide scope and high level talents in energy saving, power and environmental protection. Students have wide employment in the field of energy, environmental protection, petrochemical, aerospace, air conditioning and refrigeration and power. They can also engage in scientific research, education, management in research institution, university and government agency.
Our major is assisted by the important laboratories construction of 'The Eleventh Five-Year Plan' and 'The Twelfth Five-Year Plan' of the Ministry of Transport and the third period important disciplines construction of 'Project 211', owning Small Marine Gas Turbine Technology Key Laboratory, its professional construction scale, experimental conditions and research capabilities have reached the advanced level of similar professional universities in China.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业培养德、智、体、美、劳全面发展，具备能源与动力工程基础理论、专业知识与应用能力，能够在能源动力领域从事设计和制造、技术开发、应用研究和运行管理等方面工作，并在工程实践中遵守职业道德和规范，富有创新意识、法律意识与环境意识，具有团队精神、持续学习能力与国际视野的高素质工程技术人才。
上述培养目标可具体表述为以下四个子项：
培养目标 1：系统地掌握数学与自然科学和专业基础知识与技能，为解决能源与动力工程方面的复杂工程问题提供系统方案和工程实施；
培养目标 2：具备独立分析和解决复杂工程问题的基本能力，富有实践和创新能力，能够成为所在工作领域的专业技术骨干；
培养目标 3：具备高度的社会责任感、职业道德和创新精神，能在工程实践中考虑和评价社会、健康、安全、法律、环境及可持续发展等方面的问题；
培养目标 4：具有较强的团队协作、人际交往、组织协调和跨文化合作交流能力；具备自主和终身学习能力，不断提升自我，以适应社会经济发展的需要。
This major cultivates the comprehensive development of morality, intelligence, physical education, beauty, and labor, possesses basic theories, professional knowledge and application capabilities of energy and power engineering, and is able to engage in design and manufacturing, technology development, application research, and operation management in the field of energy and power. , And abide by professional ethics and norms in engineering practice, are full of innovative, legal and environmental awareness, have team spirit, continuous learning ability and high-quality engineering and technical personnel with an international perspective.
The above-mentioned training objectives can be specifically expressed as the following four sub-items:
Training goal 1: To systematically master basic knowledge and skills of mathematics and natural sciences and professional, to provide systematic solutions and project implementation for solving complex engineering problems in energy and power engineering;
Training goal 2: Have the basic ability to independently analyze and solve complex engineering problems, be rich in practice and innovation, and be able to become a professional and technical backbone in the field of work;
Training goal 3: Have a high sense of social responsibility, professional ethics and innovative spirit, and be able to consider and evaluate social, health, safety, legal, environmental and sustainable development issues in engineering practice;
Training goal 4: Have strong teamwork, interpersonal communication, organization and coordination and cross-cultural cooperation and communication skills; have the ability to autonomy and lifelong learning, and constantly improve themselves to meet the needs of social and economic development.
三、培养要求
III．Program Requirements
本专业学生毕业时应掌握和具备以下几方面的知识与能力：
Our Graduate Attribute Profile has 12 elements, supported by a Knowledge Profile and a definition of the Level of Problem Solving, both given below:
工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础知识和专业知识应用于能源与动力工程领域复杂工程问题的解决；
Engineering knowledge: Apply knowledge of energy and power engineering based mathematics, natural science, engineering fundamentals and an engineering specialization respectively to the solution of complex engineering problems;
问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学、工程基础和能源与动力工程基本原理以及通过文献研究来对能源与动力工程领域的复杂工程问题进行识别、表达和研究分析，以获得有效结论；
Problem analysis: Identify, formulate, describe and analysis complex engineering problems reaching substantiated conclusions using first principles of mathematics, natural sciences and energy and power engineering;
设计/开发解决方案：能够进行能源与动力工程的全周期、全流程设计，或基于工程实际问题进行工艺流程或方案设计以解决复杂能源与动力工程问题，并设计环节中体现出创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化、环境等问题；
Design/development of solutions: Design solutions for complex engineering problems and design new energy and power engineering processes that meet specified needs with appropriate consideration for public health, and safety, cultural, societal and environmental considerations;
研究：能够基于能源与动力工程基本原理并采用科学的方法通过设计、实施实验方案、分析、解释实验结果与数据对复杂的工程问题进行研究，并通过综合各方面的信息得出合理有效的结论；
Investigation: Conduct investigations of complex problems using fundamental knowledge of energy and power engineering and research methods including design of experiments, analysis and interpretation of data, and synthesis of information to provide valid conclusions.
使用现代工具：能够在解决能源与动力工程领域复杂工程问题时合理使用和开发相关的技术、资源、程序、模拟软件、分析检测仪器、工程工具和信息技术工具等，并理解其局限性；
Modern tool usage: Have the good knowledge on the techniques, resources and modern engineering and IT tools regarding to the energy and power engineering, and create, select and apply appropriate items, including prediction and modeling, to complex engineering problems;
工程与社会：能够基于能源与动力工程领域相关的工程背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任；
The engineer and society: Apply reasoning informed by energy and power engineering knowledge to assess societal, health, safety, legal and cultural issues and the consequent responsibilities relevant to material engineering practice and solutions to complex engineering problems;
环境与可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂能源与动力工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响；
Environment and sustainability: Understand and evaluate the sustainability and impact of engineering work in the solution of complex energy and power engineering problems in societal and environmental contexts;
职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在能源与动力工程领域的工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任；
Ethics: Apply ethical principles and commit to professional ethics and responsibilities and norms of energy and power engineering practice;
个人和团队：具备良好的团队合作精神与责任意识，能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色；
Individual and teamwork: Function effectively as an individual, and as a member or leader in diverse teams and in multi-disciplinary settings;
沟通：能够就能源与动力工程领域的复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流；
Communication: Communicate effectively on complex energy and power engineering problems with the engineering community and society at large, such as being able to comprehend and write effective reports and design documentation, make effective presentations and give and receive clear instructions.
项目管理：理解并掌握能源与动力工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用；
Project management and finance: Demonstrate knowledge and understanding of energy and power engineering management principles and economic decision-making and apply these to one’s own work as a member and leader in a team, to manage projects and in multi-disciplinary environments.
终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。
Life-long learning: Recognize the need for, and have the preparation and ability to engage in, independent and life-long learning in the broadest context of technological change.
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
燃气轮机原理、内燃机原理、汽轮机原理、动力机械调节与控制、动力机械强度与振动、制冷原理与设备、人工环境与空气调节、制冷装置设计与自动化、低温技术及应用、船舶制冷与空调、动力机械结构设计、新能源与可持续发展。
Theory of Gas Turbine, Principles of Internal Combustion Engine, Theory of Steam Turbine, Adjustment and Control of Power Machinery, Intensity and Vibration of Power Machinery, Refrigeration Theory and equipment, Artificial environment and air condition, Refrigeration Equipment Design and Automation, Cryogenic Refrigeration Technology & Application, Refrigeration and Air Conditioner of Marine, Structure Design of Power Mechanics, New Energy and Sustainable Development

毕业要求1 Graduation Requirement 1 工程知识：具备将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识应用于船舶与海洋工程领域复杂工程问题的能力。 Engineering knowledge: the ability to apply mathematics, natural sciences, engineering fundamentals and expertise to complex engineering issues in the field of naval architecture and ocean engineering.	1-1 能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识运用到复杂船舶与海洋工程问题的恰当表述中。 1-1 to use the mathematics, natural sciences, engineering fundamentals and expertise to the appropriate statements of complex naval architecture and ocean engineering issues.

毕业要求3 Graduation Requirement 3 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂船舶与海洋工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Design / develop solutions: Design solutions for complex naval architecture and ocean engineering problems, design systems, units (components) or processes that meet specific needs, and be able to embody innovation awareness in the design process, taking into account social, health, safety, and law, culture and environment and other factors.	3-1 能够进行复杂工程问题的针对性调研，确定设计目标。 3-1 be able to carry out complex engineering problems targeted research to determine the design goals.

毕业要求9 Graduation Requirement 9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Individuals and Teams: The ability to take on individual, team members, and responsible roles in a multidisciplinary team.	9-1 具有团队协作意识，具有一定的组织管理能力和较强的自我控制能力、人际交往能力。 9-1 have a sense of teamwork, with a certain degree of organizational management and strong self-control, interpersonal skills.

毕业要求9 Graduation Requirement 9 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Individuals and Teams: The ability to take on individual, team members, and responsible roles in a multidisciplinary team.	9-3 具有跨领域的综合能力，了解与本专业相关学科等领域的技术衔接，具备整合工程应用中所涉及相关学科的综合能力。 9-3 the comprehensive ability of cross-field, understand related disciplines and other areas of technical convergence, with the integration of engineering applications involved in the relevant disciplines of comprehensive ability.
毕业要求10 Graduation Requirement 10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 Communication: The ability to communicate and discuss effectively with industry peers and the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and design submissions, making statements, expressing clearly or responding to directives. And have a certain international perspective, to communicate and discuss in cross-cultural background.	10-1 能够通过口头、书面、图表、工程图纸等方式表达思想，与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流。 10-1  to express ideas through oral, written, charts, engineering drawings, etc., and communicate and discuss effectively with industry peers and the public.
毕业要求10 Graduation Requirement 10 沟通：能够就复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 Communication: The ability to communicate and discuss effectively with industry peers and the public on complex engineering issues, including writing reports and design submissions, making statements, expressing clearly or responding to directives. And have a certain international perspective, to communicate and discuss in cross-cultural background.	10-2 能够采用一门外国语言，在跨文化背景下进行沟通交流。 10-2 be able to use a foreign language to communicate in the context of cross-cultural.

毕业要求11 Graduation Requirement 11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 Project management: To understand and master the principles of project management and economic decision-making methods, and can be applied in a multi-disciplinary environment.	11-1 能够对船舶与海洋工程项目的工艺路线、工艺方案进行技术经济分析和比较。 11-1 do technical and economic analysis and have comparison of the technological route and process plan of naval architecture and ocean engineering project.
毕业要求11 Graduation Requirement 11 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 Project management: To understand and master the principles of project management and economic decision-making methods, and can be applied in a multi-disciplinary environment.	11-2 了解船舶与海洋工程项目的实施过程，掌握工程项目运营的相关技术与管理知识。 11-2 understand the naval architecture and ocean engineering project implementation process, master the related technology and management knowledge of engineering project operation.
毕业要求12 Graduation Requirement 12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 Lifelong learning: with independent learning and lifelong learning awareness, have the ability to continue to learn and adapt to development.	12-1 具有自主学习和终身学习意识，具备终身学习的知识基础，掌握自主学习的方法，了解拓展知识和能力的途径。 12-1  with independent learning and lifelong learning awareness, with a lifelong learning knowledge base, master the way of self-learning, understanding of ways to expand knowledge and ability.
毕业要求12 Graduation Requirement 12 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 Lifelong learning: with independent learning and lifelong learning awareness, have the ability to continue to learn and adapt to development.	12-2 能针对个人或职业发展需求，采用合适的方法，自主学习，适应船舶与海洋工程领域的发展。 12-2 for personal or career development needs, to use appropriate methods to go on self-learning and adapt to the development of naval architecture and ocean engineering field.

1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 ，需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 毕 业 要 求Graduation Requirement	毕 业 要 求 观 测 点 分 解Points of Observation for Graduation
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决机械领域复杂工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。 Graduation Requirement 1 Engineering knowledge：master mathematics, natural science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge and their application to solve complex engineering problems in mechanical field.	1-1能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识运用到机械领域复杂工程问题的恰当表述中。 1-1 Be able to apply mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals and expertise to the appropriate presentation of complex engineering problems in the mechanical field.
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决机械领域复杂工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。 Graduation Requirement 1 Engineering knowledge：master mathematics, natural science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge and their application to solve complex engineering problems in mechanical field.	1-2能针对一个系统或过程，建立合适的数学模型，并利用恰当的边界条件求解。 1-2 Can establish a suitable mathematical model for a system or process, and use appropriate boundary conditions to solve it.
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决机械领域复杂工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。 Graduation Requirement 1 Engineering knowledge：master mathematics, natural science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge and their application to solve complex engineering problems in mechanical field.	1-3能够将相关知识和数学模型方法用于分析、判别机械工程问题。 1-3 Be able to apply knowledge and mathematical modeling methods to analyze and identify mechanical engineering problems.
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决机械领域复杂工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。 Graduation Requirement 1 Engineering knowledge：master mathematics, natural science, engineering fundamentals and professional knowledge and their application to solve complex engineering problems in mechanical field.	1-4能够将相关知识和数学模型方法用于专业工程问题解决方案的比较与综合。 1-4 Be able to compare and synthesize solutions to professional engineering problems using relevant knowledge and mathematical modeling methods.
毕业要求2问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析机械领域复杂工程问题，以获得有效结论。 Graduation Requirement 2 Problem analysis: be able to apply basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to identify, express, and analyze complex engineering problems in the mechanical field through literature research to reach effective conclusions.	2-1能够根据工程情景，运用数学、自然科学、工程科学等相关科学原理，识别和判断复杂机械设计制造工程问题的关键因素。 2-1 Be able to identify and judge the key factors of complex problems in mechanical design and manufacturing engineering based on engineering situations and relevant scientific principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science.
毕业要求2问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析机械领域复杂工程问题，以获得有效结论。 Graduation Requirement 2 Problem analysis: be able to apply basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to identify, express, and analyze complex engineering problems in the mechanical field through literature research to reach effective conclusions.	2-2能基于相关科学原理和数学模型方法，正确表达机械领域复杂工程问题。 2-2 Be able to correctly express complex engineering problems in mechanical field based on relevant scientific principles and mathematical model methods.
毕业要求2问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析机械领域复杂工程问题，以获得有效结论。 Graduation Requirement 2 Problem analysis: be able to apply basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to identify, express, and analyze complex engineering problems in the mechanical field through literature research to reach effective conclusions.	2-3能够运用相关科学原理和数学模型方法，结合文献研究，比较解决问题的多种方案，并对机械领域复杂工程问题的影响因素进行分析，获得有效结论。 2-3 Can use relevant scientific principles and mathematical modelling methods, combined with literature research, compare various solutions to solve problems and analyze the influencing factors of complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, and obtain effective conclusions.
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对机械领域复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Graduation Requirement 3 Design/development solutions: be able to design solutions to complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, design systems, units (components) or processes to meet specific requirements, and be innovative in the design process, considering social, health, safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors.	3-1能够对机械领域复杂工程问题进行方案设计。 3-1 Be able to design solutions for complex engineering problems in mechanical field.
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对机械领域复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Graduation Requirement 3 Design/development solutions: be able to design solutions to complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, design systems, units (components) or processes to meet specific requirements, and be innovative in the design process, considering social, health, safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors.	3-2能够根据解决方案对特定需求的典型机械产品、零部件、传动与控制和机械制造过程进行设计。 3-2 Be able to design typical machine products, parts, drives and controls, and machine manufacturing processes for specific requirements according to solutions.
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对机械领域复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Graduation Requirement 3 Design/development solutions: be able to design solutions to complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, design systems, units (components) or processes to meet specific requirements, and be innovative in the design process, considering social, health, safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors.	3-3能够在机械系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程等设计环节中体现创新意识。 3-3 Be able to demonstrate innovation in the design of mechanical systems, units or processes.
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对机械领域复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Graduation Requirement 3 Design/development solutions: be able to design solutions to complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, design systems, units (components) or processes to meet specific requirements, and be innovative in the design process, considering social, health, safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors.	3-4在解决机械工程问题的设计环节中，能够考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 3-4 Consider social, health, safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors in the design process of solving mechanical engineering problems.
毕业要求4研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对机械领域复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 Graduation Requirement 4 Research: be able to conduct research on complex engineering problems in mechanical field based on scientific principles and methods, including designing conducting, analyzing and interpreting data, and obtaining reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis.	4-1 能够基于科学原理，运用文献研究或相关方法，进行机械领域复杂工程问题解决方案的调研和分析。 4-1 Be able to investigate and analyze solutions to complex engineering problems in mechanical field based on scientific principles and literature research or related methods.
毕业要求4研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对机械领域复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 Graduation Requirement 4 Research: be able to conduct research on complex engineering problems in mechanical field based on scientific principles and methods, including designing conducting, analyzing and interpreting data, and obtaining reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis.	4-2能够运用所学科学原理并采用科学方法，针对机械领域复杂工程问题设计实验方案，建立实验系统，安全地开展实验并正确地采集实验数据。 4-2 Be able to comprehensively apply the scientific principles and adopt scientific methods to design experimental schemes for complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, establish experimental systems, safely carry out experiments and correctly collect experimental data.
毕业要求4研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对机械领域复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 Graduation Requirement 4 Research: be able to conduct research on complex engineering problems in mechanical field based on scientific principles and methods, including designing conducting, analyzing and interpreting data, and obtaining reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis.	4-3基于科学理论，对实验数据和结果进行分析和解释，并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 4-3 Be able to analyze and explain the experimental data and results based on scientific theory, and obtain reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis.
毕业要求5使用现代工具：能够针对机械领域复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对机械领域复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 Graduation Requirement 5 Use of modern tools: develop, select and use appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, including prediction and simulation of complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, and understand their limitations.	5-1了解专业常用的现代仪器、信息技术工具、工程工具和模拟软件等现代工具的使用原理、方法和局限性，能够针对机械领域复杂工程问题，选择和使用恰当的现代工具等进行分析、计算与设计。 5-1 Understand the principles, methods and limitations of modern tools such as modern instruments, information technology tools, engineering tools and simulation software, and be able to analyze, calculate and design complex engineering problems in the mechanical field by selecting and using appropriate modern tools.
毕业要求5使用现代工具：能够针对机械领域复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对机械领域复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 Graduation Requirement 5 Use of modern tools: develop, select and use appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, including prediction and simulation of complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, and understand their limitations.	5-2能够针对机械领域复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的现代工具进行建模、预测与仿真，并能够理解相关工具的局限性。 5-2 Be able to develop, select and use appropriate modern tools for modeling, predicting and simulation of complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, and understand the limitations of relevant tools.
毕业要求6工程与社会：能够基于机械工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 Graduation Requirement 6 Engineering and society: be able to conduct rational analysis based on mechanical engineering background, evaluate the social, health, safety, legal and cultural impact of engineering practices and solutions to complex engineering problems, and understand their responsibilities.	6-1了解机械工程领域的技术标准体系、知识产权、产业政策和法律法规，理解不同社会文化对机械工程活动的影响。 6-1 Understand the technical standards system, intellectual property rights, industrial policies and laws and regulations in the field of mechanical engineering, and understand the influence of different social cultures on mechanical engineering activities.
毕业要求6工程与社会：能够基于机械工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 Graduation Requirement 6 Engineering and society: be able to conduct rational analysis based on mechanical engineering background, evaluate the social, health, safety, legal and cultural impact of engineering practices and solutions to complex engineering problems, and understand their responsibilities.	6-2能分析和评价机械工程实践和机械领域复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律、文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 6-2 Be able to analyze and evaluate the social, health, safety, legal and cultural impacts of mechanical engineering practices and solutions to complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, and understand their responsibilities.
毕业要求7环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对机械领域复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 Graduation Requirement 7 Environment and sustainability: be able to understand and evaluate the impact of engineering practices of complex engineering problems in the mechanical field on environmental and social sustainability.	7-1理解机械工程实践中环境保护和社会可持续发展的理念和内涵。 7-1 Understand the concept and connotation of environmental protection and social sustainable development in mechanical engineering practice.
毕业要求7环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对机械领域复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 Graduation Requirement 7 Environment and sustainability: be able to understand and evaluate the impact of engineering practices of complex engineering problems in the mechanical field on environmental and social sustainability.	7-2能根据环境和社会可持续发展原则，评价机械领域复杂工程问题的工程实践对环境和社会可持续发展的影响。 7-2 Be able to evaluate the impact of engineering practice of complex engineering problems in mechanical field on environmental and social sustainable development according to the principles of environmental and social sustainable development.
毕业要求8职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在机械工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Graduation Requirement 8 Professional norms: possess humanistic and social science literacy and social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in mechanical engineering practice, and perform responsibilities.	8-1了解中国国情，理解个人与社会的关系，树立社会主义核心价值观，具有民族复兴和社会进步的责任感。 8-1 Understand China's national conditions, understand the relationship between individuals and society, establish socialist core values, and have a sense of responsibility for national rejuvenation and social progress.
毕业要求8职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在机械工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Graduation Requirement 8 Professional norms: possess humanistic and social science literacy and social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in mechanical engineering practice, and perform responsibilities.	8-2在工程实践中遵守机械工程师的职业道德和行为规范。 8-2 Abide by the professional ethics and code of conduct of mechanical engineer in engineering practice.
毕业要求8职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在机械工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Graduation Requirement 8 Professional norms: possess humanistic and social science literacy and social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in mechanical engineering practice, and perform responsibilities.	8-3能够在工程实践中，自觉履行机械工程师对公众的安全、健康和福祉，以及环境保护的社会责任。 8-3 Be able to consciously fulfill the social responsibility of mechanical engineer for public safety, health and well-being, and environmental protection in engineering practice.
毕业要求9个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Graduation Requirement 9 Individuals and teams: be able to take on individual, team member and leader roles in a multi-disciplinary team setting.	9-1能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担任务，并独立完成。 9-1 Be able to work in a multi-disciplinary team and work independently.
毕业要求9个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Graduation Requirement 9 Individuals and teams: be able to take on individual, team member and leader roles in a multi-disciplinary team setting.	9-2能够与团队成员沟通合作，分享成果。 9-2 Be able to communicate and collaborate with team members and share results.
毕业要求9个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Graduation Requirement 9 Individuals and teams: be able to take on individual, team member and leader roles in a multi-disciplinary team setting.	9-3具有团队组织管理能力，能够合理分配团队成员任务。 9-3 Have the ability of team organization and management, be able to reasonably assign tasks to team members.
毕业要求10沟通：能够就机械领域复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 Graduation Requirement 10 Communication: be able to effectively communicate with industry peers and the public on complex engineering issues in the mechanical field, including writing reports and instructions, making presentations, clearly expressing or responding to instructions. And have a certain international vision, can communicate and exchange in the cross-cultural background.	10-1了解专业领域发展趋势，能够撰写机械工程问题的专业论文、技术报告和设计方案等技术文件。 10-1 Understand the development trend of the professional field, and be able to write professional papers, technical reports and instructions on mechanical engineering problems.
毕业要求10沟通：能够就机械领域复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 Graduation Requirement 10 Communication: be able to effectively communicate with industry peers and the public on complex engineering issues in the mechanical field, including writing reports and instructions, making presentations, clearly expressing or responding to instructions. And have a certain international vision, can communicate and exchange in the cross-cultural background.	10-2能够与业界同行及社会公众交流沟通，就机械领域复杂工程问题进行陈述发言，清晰表达研究或设计的具体思想、思路、方案、所采取的措施和效果等。 10-2 be able to communicate with peers in the industry and the public, make statements on complex engineering problems in the mechanical field, clearly express specific ideas, ideas, schemes, measures and effects of research or design, etc.
毕业要求10沟通：能够就机械领域复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 Graduation Requirement 10 Communication: be able to effectively communicate with industry peers and the public on complex engineering issues in the mechanical field, including writing reports and instructions, making presentations, clearly expressing or responding to instructions. And have a certain international vision, can communicate and exchange in the cross-cultural background.	10-3掌握一门外语，能就专业问题，在跨文化背景下进行基本沟通和交流。 10-3 Master a foreign language, and be able to conduct basic communications on professional issues in a cross-cultural context.
毕业要求11项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 Graduation Requirement 11 Project management: understand and master engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods and can apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-1理解并掌握工程活动涉及的工程管理和经济学基本知识。 11-1 Understand and master basic knowledge of engineering management and economics related to engineering activities.
毕业要求11项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 Graduation Requirement 11 Project management: understand and master engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods and can apply them in a multidisciplinary environment.	11-2能够在多学科环境下，就机械工程问题合理应用工程管理原理与经济决策方法。 11-2 Be able to apply engineering management principles and economic decision-making methods to mechanical engineering problems in a multidisciplinary environment.
毕业要求12具终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 Graduation Requirement 12 Lifelong learning: have the consciousness of independent learning and lifelong learning, have the ability of continuous learning and adapting to development.	12-1能在社会发展的大背景下，具有自主学习和终身学习的意识。 12-1 Possess the awareness of independent learning and lifelong learning in the context of social development.
毕业要求12具终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 Graduation Requirement 12 Lifelong learning: have the consciousness of independent learning and lifelong learning, have the ability of continuous learning and adapting to development.	12-2针对机械工程问题的复杂性，掌握自主学习的方法，具有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 12-2 In view of the complexity of mechanical engineering problems, master the method of independent learning, and have the ability of continuous learning and adapting to development.

1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 ，需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决救助与打捞工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-1能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识运用到复杂救助与打捞工程问题的恰当表述中。
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决救助与打捞工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-2能针对一个系统或过程，建立合适的数学模型，并利用恰当的边界条件求解。
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决救助与打捞工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-3能够将相关知识和数学模型方法用于分析、判别救助与打捞工程问题。
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决救助与打捞工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-4能够将相关知识和数学模型方法用于专业工程问题解决方案的比较与综合。
毕业要求2问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂救助与打捞工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-1能够根据工程情景，运用相关科学知识，结合文献研究，识别和判断救助与打捞工程问题关键因素。
毕业要求2问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂救助与打捞工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-2能够运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，建立救助与打捞工程问题的模型，进行问题的表达。
毕业要求2问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂救助与打捞工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-3能够综合运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，并结合文献研究，对复杂救助与打捞工程问题进行分析，以获得有效结论。
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的装备、系统或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-1能够对特定需求的救助过程、打捞过程、海洋工程施工过程等复杂救助与打捞工程问题进行方案设计。
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的装备、系统或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-2能够根据解决方案对特定需求的典型救助装备、打捞装备、救助与打捞工艺进行设计。
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的装备、系统或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-3 具有追求创新的意识，能够在设计环节中进行创新。
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的装备、系统或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-4在解决救助与打捞工程问题的设计环节中，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。
毕业要求4研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂救助与打捞工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-1 能够基于科学原理，运用文献研究或相关方法，进行复杂救助与打捞工程问题解决方案的调研。
毕业要求4研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂救助与打捞工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-2能够综合运用所学科学原理并采用科学方法，针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题设计实验方案，建立实验系统，按照合理步骤进行实验并获取数据。
毕业要求4研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂救助与打捞工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-3基于科学理论，对实验数据和结果进行分析和解释，获得合理有效的结论。
毕业要求5使用现代工具：能够针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。	5-1了解常用的现代工具使用原理和方法，能够针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题，选择和使用恰当的技术、资源、现代信息技术工具等进行分析、计算与设计，获得所需的相关资料。
毕业要求5使用现代工具：能够针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。	5-2能够针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的现代工程工具进行建模、预测与仿真，并能够理解相关工具的局限性。
毕业要求6工程与社会：能够基于救助与打捞工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。	6-1了解救助与打捞工程的发展历史、文化背景和政策法规知识，理解救助与打捞工程对客观世界和社会的影响及其应承担的责任。
毕业要求6工程与社会：能够基于救助与打捞工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。	6-2能分析和评价救助打捞工程实践和复杂救助打捞工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律、文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。
毕业要求7环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。	7-1理解救助与打捞工程实践对环境保护、社会和谐和可持续发展的影响内涵。
毕业要求7环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂救助与打捞工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。	7-2能根据环境和社会可持续发展原则，综合评价复杂救助与打捞工程问题的工程实践对环境和社会可持续发展的影响。
毕业要求8职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在救助与打捞工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。	8-1了解中国国情，理解个人与社会的关系，树立社会主义核心价值观，具有民族复兴和社会进步的责任感。
毕业要求8职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在救助与打捞工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。	8-2在工程实践中遵守救助打捞卓越工程师的职业道德和行为规范。
毕业要求8职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在救助与打捞工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。	8-3能够在工程实践中，自觉履行救助打捞卓越工程师对公众的安全、健康和福祉，以及环境保护的社会责任。
毕业要求9个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。	9-1能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担任务，并独立完成。
毕业要求9个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。	9-2能够与团队成员沟通合作，分享成果。
毕业要求9个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。	9-3具有团队组织管理能力，能够合理分配团队成员任务。
毕业要求10沟通：能够就复杂救助与打捞工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。	10-1了解专业领域发展趋势，能够撰写救助与打捞工程问题的专业论文、技术报告和设计方案等技术文件。
毕业要求10沟通：能够就复杂救助与打捞工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。	10-2能够与业界同行及社会公众交流沟通，就复杂救助与打捞工程问题进行陈述发言，清晰表达研究或设计的具体思想、思路、方案、所采取的措施和效果等。
毕业要求10沟通：能够就复杂救助与打捞工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。	10-3掌握一门外语，能就专业问题，在跨文化背景下进行基本沟通和交流。
毕业要求11项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。	11-1理解并掌握工程活动涉及的工程管理和经济学基本知识。
毕业要求11项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。	11-2能够在多学科环境下，就救助与打捞工程问题合理应用工程管理原理与经济决策方法。
毕业要求12具终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。	12-1具有不断汲取新知识、掌握新技术、与时俱进的学习意识。
毕业要求12具终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。	12-2针对工程问题的复杂性，掌握自主学习的方法，具有不断学习和适应发展的能力。

毕 业 要 求	毕 业 要 求 指 标 点 分 解
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决能源与动力工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-1能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识运用到复杂能源与动力工程问题的恰当表述中。
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决能源与动力工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-2能针对一个系统或过程，建立合适的数学模型，并利用恰当的边界条件求解。
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决能源与动力工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-3能够将相关知识和数学模型方法用于分析、判别能源与动力工程问题。
毕业要求1工程知识：具备用于解决能源与动力工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-4能够将相关知识和数学模型方法用于专业工程问题解决方案的比较与综合。
毕业要求2问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂能源与动力工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-1能够根据工程情景，运用相关科学知识，结合文献研究，识别和判断能源与动力工程问题关键因素。
毕业要求2问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂能源与动力工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-2能够运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，建立能源与动力工程问题的模型，进行问题的表达。
毕业要求2问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂能源与动力工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-3能够综合运用数学、自然科学、工程科学的基本原理和方法，并结合文献研究，对复杂能源与动力工程问题进行分析，以获得有效结论。
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂能源与动力工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的装备、系统或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-1掌握能源动力及相关领域复杂工程设计和产品开发全周期、全流程的基本方法和技术，掌握影响设计目标和技术方案的各种因素。
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂能源与动力工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的装备、系统或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-2能够根据解决方案对特定需求的典型新技术、新工艺和新产品进行设计、研究和开发。
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂能源与动力工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的装备、系统或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-3 具有追求创新的意识，能够在设计环节中进行创新。
毕业要求3设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂能源与动力工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的装备、系统或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-4在解决能源与动力工程问题的设计环节中，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。
毕业要求4研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂能源与动力工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-1 能够基于科学原理，运用文献研究或相关方法，进行复杂能源与动力工程问题解决方案的调研。
毕业要求4研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂能源与动力工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-2能够综合运用所学科学原理并采用科学方法，针对复杂能源与动力工程问题设计实验方案，建立实验系统，按照合理步骤进行实验并获取数据。
毕业要求4研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂能源与动力工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-3基于科学理论，对实验数据和结果进行分析和解释，获得合理有效的结论。
毕业要求5使用现代工具：能够针对复杂能源与动力工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。	5-1了解常用的现代工具使用原理和方法，能够针对复杂能源与动力工程问题，选择和使用恰当的技术、资源、现代信息技术工具等进行分析、计算与设计，获得所需的相关资料。
毕业要求5使用现代工具：能够针对复杂能源与动力工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。	5-2能够针对复杂能源与动力工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的现代工程工具进行建模、预测与仿真，并能够理解相关工具的局限性。
毕业要求6工程与社会：能够基于能源与动力工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。	6-1了解能源与动力工程的发展历史、文化背景和政策法规知识，理解能源与动力工程对客观世界和社会的影响及其应承担的责任。
毕业要求6工程与社会：能够基于能源与动力工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。	6-2能分析和评价能源动力工程实践和复杂能源动力工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律、文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。
毕业要求7环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂能源与动力工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。	7-1理解能源与动力工程实践对环境保护、社会和谐和可持续发展的影响内涵。
毕业要求7环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂能源与动力工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。	7-2能根据环境和社会可持续发展原则，综合评价复杂能源与动力工程问题的工程实践对环境和社会可持续发展的影响。
毕业要求8职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在能源与动力工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。	8-1了解中国国情，理解个人与社会的关系，树立社会主义核心价值观，具有民族复兴和社会进步的责任感。
毕业要求8职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在能源与动力工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。	8-2在工程实践中遵守工程师的职业道德和行为规范。
毕业要求8职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在能源与动力工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。	8-3能够在工程实践中，自觉履行工程师对公众的安全、健康和福祉，以及环境保护的社会责任。
毕业要求9个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。	9-1能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担任务，并独立完成。
毕业要求9个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。	9-2能够与团队成员沟通合作，分享成果。
毕业要求9个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。	9-3具有团队组织管理能力，能够合理分配团队成员任务。
毕业要求10沟通：能够就复杂能源与动力工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。	10-1了解专业领域发展趋势，能够撰写能源与动力工程问题的专业论文、技术报告和设计方案等技术文件。
毕业要求10沟通：能够就复杂能源与动力工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。	10-2能够与业界同行及社会公众交流沟通，就复杂能源与动力工程问题进行陈述发言，清晰表达研究或设计的具体思想、思路、方案、所采取的措施和效果等。
毕业要求10沟通：能够就复杂能源与动力工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。	10-3掌握一门外语，能就专业问题，在跨文化背景下进行基本沟通和交流。
毕业要求11项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。	11-1理解并掌握工程活动涉及的工程管理和经济学基本知识。
毕业要求11项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。	11-2能够在多学科环境下，就能源与动力工程问题合理应用工程管理原理与经济决策方法。
毕业要求12具终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。	12-1具有不断汲取新知识、掌握新技术、与时俱进的学习意识。
毕业要求12具终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。	12-2针对工程问题的复杂性，掌握自主学习的方法，具有不断学习和适应发展的能力。

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits.
